    SELECT TOP(1) [u].[Id], [u].[ActiveToken], [u].[Email], [u].[FirstName], [u].[HashedPassword], [u].[IsActive], [u].[LastName], [u].[ProfileImage], [u].[RegisterDate], [u].[RoleId], [u].[Username], [r].[Id] AS [Id0], [r].[Title]
    FROM [Users] AS [u]
    INNER JOIN [Roles] AS [r] ON [u].[RoleId] = [r].[Id]
    WHERE [u].[Username] = @__decodedJWTModel_Username_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN [Wallpapers] AS [w] ON [t].[Id] = [w].[UploaderId]
LEFT JOIN [Wallpapers] AS [w0] ON [t].[Id] = [w0].[UserId]
LEFT JOIN [Likes] AS [l] ON [t].[Id] = [l].[LikerId]
ORDER BY [t].[Id], [t].[Id0], [w].[Id], [w0].[Id]
